1a1(1): dpal he ru ka snying rje rol pa'i rgyud gsang ba zab mo'i mchog ces bya ba bzhugs so//
1b1(1): rgya gar skad du/ shrI he ru ka kA ru Na krI Di ta ta na tra gu h+ya gaM b+hi ra u ta ta ma nA ma/ bod skad du/ dpal he ru ka snying rje rol pa'i rgyud gsang ba zab mo'i mchog ces bya
1b2(1): ba// dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dang / rdo rje dang / rin po che dang / pad+ma
1b3(1): dang / las kyi rigs thams cad kyi mchog tu gsang ba chen po dam tshig gi sdom pa gnyis su med pa'i bde ba chen po dbang brnyes pa/ thabs dang shes rab kyi rnal 'byor gyi dbang
1b4(1): phyug chen po/ khams gsum thams cad kyi bdag po chen po/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchog tu gsang ba chen po nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du mnyam par 'jug pa/
2a1(1): pha rol tu phyin pa'i skabs dang ldan pa/ che mchog he ru ka'i shes rab dang ye shes kyi dbang bskur ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs
2a2(1): rin po che gsang ba rdo rje gsang ba'i bcom ldan 'das bud med kyi dkyil na gsung brjod pa med par bzhugs so// sangs rgyas kyi zhing nam mkha'i dbyings kyi rdul phran dang mnyam
2a3(1): pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dang / rdo rje nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ba chen mo dang / skal ba dang ldan pa dang / 'jib par byed pa'i gsang ba
2a4(1): chen mo'i g.yog dang / 'byung ba chen po lnga dang / 'byung ba las gyur pa'i lha'i tshogs 'bum phrag brgya stong gis khyab pa 'di lta ste/ snying po ye shes rdo rje dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi ye
2b1(1): shes rdo rje dang me long ye shes rdo rje dang / so sor kun tu rtog pa'i ye shes rdo rje dang / mnyam pa nyid ye shes rdo rje dang / bya ba nan tan ye shes rdo rje dang / nam mkha' ye shes rdo rje dang / rlung ye shes rdo rje dang /
2b2(1): me ye shes rdo rje dang / chu ye shes rdo rje dang / sa ye shes rdo rje dang / thabs dang shes rab ye shes rdo rje dang / gzugs ye shes rdo rje dang / sgra ye shes rdo rje dang / dri ye shes rdo rje dang / ro ye shes rdo rje dang /
2b3(1): reg ye shes rdo rje dang / sku ye shes rdo rje dang / gsung ye shes rdo rje dang / thugs ye shes rdo rje dang / bde ba chen po ye shes rdo rje dang / kun du bzang po ye shes rdo rje dang / gsung gi dbang po ye shes rdo rje dang /
2b4(1): gnyis su med pa'i ye shes rdo rje dang / zhi ba'i ye shes rdo rje dang / gdul dka' 'dul ba'i ye shes rdo rje dang / rgyal ba'i ye shes rdo rje dang / me tog gi ye shes rdo rje dang / rab tu dga' ba'i ye shes rdo rje dang /
2b5(1): dbang gi ye shes rdo rje dang / nyi ma'i khro bo ye shes rdo rje dang / rgyal mtshan ye shes rdo rje dang / rdo rje sgra ye shes rdo rje dang / 'gro ba 'dul ba ye shes rdo rje dang / gzhon nu ye shes rdo rje dang / rgyu ye shes rdo rje dang /
2b6(1): gsung med pa'i ye shes rdo rje dang / sna tshogs kyi ye shes rdo rje dang / go cha ye shes rdo rje dang / yang dag par zab par byed pa'i ye shes rdo rje dang / 'dus pa'i ye shes rdo rje dang / bde ba chen po'i ye shes rdo rje
3a1(1): dang / byang chub sems ye shes rdo rje dang / rin chen dbang bskur ba ye shes rdo rje dang / pad+mo dmar po ye shes rdo rje dang / dam tshig ye shes rdo rje dang / mchod pa'i ye shes rdo rje dang / rnal 'byor
3a2(1): ma chen mo g.yog dang bcas pa rnams la 'di lta ste/ shin tu dga' ba'i dbang mo zhes bya ba'i ye shes rdo rje dang / rmongs par byed pa'i dbang mo ye shes rdo rje dang / gsod ces bya ba'i dbang mo ye shes rdo rje dang /
3a3(1): rdo rje dbyings phyug ma ye shes rdo rje dang / ye shes dbyings phyug ma ye shes rdo rje dang / rin chen dbyings phyug ma ye shes rdo rje dang / pad+ma'i dbyings phyug ma ye shes rdo rje dang / las kyi dbyings phyug ma ye shes rdo
3a4(1): rje dang / gnon par byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / 'dzums par byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / rmongs par byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / rgyas 'debs par byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / 'dren par byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang /
3a5(1): gsod par byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / 'bigs par byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / gcod par byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / sdigs byed ces bya ba ye shes rdo rje dang / tshig byed ces bya ba ye shes rdo rje dang / yan
3a6(1): lag thams cad 'phrog byed ye shes rdo rje dang / 'jib byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / khrag la dga' ma ye shes rdo rje dang / gcod byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / pham byed ma ye shes rdo rje dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ma
3b1(1): ye shes rdo rje dang / ngag 'phrog ma ye shes rdo rje dang / zas sha rlon za ba ye shes rdo rje dang / srin mo ye shes rdo rje dang / gnod sbyin ma ye shes rdo rje dang / gnod byed ces bya ba ye shes rdo rje dang / sbrul ye shes
3b2(1): rdo rje dang / seng ge ye shes rdo rje dang / stag ye shes rdo rje dang / ri dwags ye shes rdo rje dang / phag ye shes rdo rje dang / spre'u ye shes rdo rje dang / khyi ye shes rdo rje dang / byi la ye shes rdo rje dang / ra ye shes rdo rje
3b3(1): dang / bya rog ye shes rdo rje dang / wa ye shes rdo rje dang / bya rgod ye shes rdo rje dang / sre mo ye shes rdo rje dang / mi'i keng rus dang / 'bu chen po'i ro dang // yi dwags dang / sha za dang / gzig dang / bong bu dang /
3b4(1): rta dang / ma he dang / ba lang dang / 'ug pa dang / rdo rje 'phrog par byed ma chen mo dang / rdo rje zas 'dren ma chen mo dang / de la sogs te mtha' yas mchog mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa dang bcas pa/ chos kyi
3b5(1): dbyings rdo rje nam mkha' la 'gro ma'i tshogs g.yog dang bcas pa/ rdo rje'i rigs ye shes rdo rje dang / ye shes kyi khro bo ye shes rdo rje dang / ye shes kyi khro mo ye shes rdo rje dang / sprul pa'i ye shes rdo rje dang / sprul
3b6(1): pa'i phra men ma ye shes rdo rje dang / yang sbrul ma chen mo ye shes rdo rje dang / bdud rtsi lha mo ye shes rdo rje dang / de dag la sogs te bye ba phrag brgya stong po rnams sgra ca co 'byin cing nam mkha' dbyings rab 'byam
4a1(1): chen po'i tshogs rnams kyis mchod par byed cing / bud med kyi dkyil na gsung brjod pa med par bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal che mchog he ru ka kun du bzang po dpal rdo rje
4a2(1): sems dpa' shin tu dgyes pa gdon mi za ba'i tshogs rdo rje gtong ba dbang mo zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ rnam pa sna tshogs kyi rol pa chen pos rnam par rol pa/ sprul pa chen po'i gar
4a3(1): dang / glu dang / sil snyan dang / gzugs dang / sgra dang / dri dang / ro dang / reg pa'i bde ba chen po dang 'phags par 'gyur ba dang / rol pa la sogs pa'i reg pa bde ba la spyod pa'i gar nye bar ston cing /
4a4(1): rnam pa sna tshogs kyi tshogs kyi tshul chen po 'phags par 'gyur ba dang / rnam pa sna tshogs kyis gnon pa dang / rnam pa sna tshogs kyis spros pa dang / gar byed pa dang / za bar byed pa dang / 'jib par byed pa
4a5(1): dang / spras par byed pa dang / zlog par byed pa dang / myong bar byed pa dang / 'gyur bar byed pa dang / 'phrog par byed pa dang / rtsom par byed pa dang / kun du 'debs par byed pa dang / bde ba nye bar stobs
4a6(1): shing reg pa ro'i bye brag mang po bye ba phrag brgya stong tshad med par nam mkha'i dbyings rdul phran las 'das par mnyam par 'jog pas nye bar gnas shing 'tsho skyong ste/ 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar
4b1(1): byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mi gzigs/ dgongs pa nye bar mi 'jog/ thabs dang shes rab ston par mi mdzad/ shin tu 'gal ba phyin ci log pa la 'jog par mi mdzad/ nye bar 'jog par
4b2(1): mi mdzad/ ma dad pa rnams dad par yang mi mdzad/ ma dul pa rnam dul bar yang mi mdzad/ nye bar gtses pa rnams 'tshe ba zhi bar yang mi mdzad/ ma 'gags pa rnams 'gog par yang mi mdzad/ ma bskul ba
4b3(1): rnams bskul bar yang mi mdzad/ ma rgyas pa rnams rgyas par yang mi mdzad/ rnam par rmongs pa rnams sel bar yang mi mdzad/ dga' bar 'gyur ba rnams mi dga' bar yang mi mdzad/ dga' bar ma gyur pa
4b4(1): rnams dga' bar yang mi mdzad/ ma khros pa rnams khros par yang mi mdzad/ mi gdug pa gdug par yang mi mdzad/ 'jigs byed chen po dang / drag po ma rungs pa chen po dang / gtum po chen po dang / lha dang
4b5(1): lha ma yin dang / log 'dren dang / gdug pa chen po dang / yi dwags dang / sha za dang / gnod sbyin dang / srin po dang / shin tu gdug pa'i gdug pa chen po dang / tsha ba'i don dang / nad dang / sbrul dang /
4b6(1): sems can thams cad la 'tshe bar byed pa rnams nye bar zhi bar yang mi mdzad/ rnam par dul bar yang mi mdzad/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'dus nas dgongs pa nye bar bzhag ste/ spyan gnyis
5a1(1): mi 'dzums par gzigs nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po la bskor zhing sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje'i phyag gis phyag byas nas// de bzhin
5a2(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje chen po'i dbyangs kyis bskul zhing gsol ba btab po// rdo rje sems dpa' sangs rgyas kun// rnam dag sras bcas byang chub rnams// yun ring bsgoms nas shin tu
5a3(1): gdungs// dga' ba'i yid kyis dgyes par mdzod// kye 'dod chags dri med kun du bzang po'i spyod pa ste// 'dod chags dam tshig la ni phye mdzad nas// dka' ba drug spyad shin tu gsungs pa yis// 'dod pa
5a4(1): bde ba nyid kyis 'jig par mdzod// rnam dag rdo rje las byung ye shes chu// rin chen 'bar ba'i byang chub sems ni rab phyung nas// rgyal ba thams cad rnams kyi dbu ni skams pa la// dri med rin chen char
5a5(1): gyis spyi bor dbang bskur mdzod// mnyam dang mi mnyam 'dod chags tshul dag pa// pad+ma'i gnas su rdo rje mdzod gtod pas// sna tshogs sems dpa' sems brlan brlag gyur pas// sbyor ba gzhan min ma
5a6(1): rtogs bshad du gsol// rdo rje sems khyod dbang mchog bde ba byed pa'i mchog/ rdo rje pad+mo dbye ba'i tshul gyis sbyor mdzod de// rgyal ba kun gyi gzugs kyi sku ni rab btud nas// thams cad bde ba'i sgrub pa
5b1(1): nyid kyis mnyes par mdzod// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kun du dpal rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbyangs kyis nges par bskul ba thugs su chud
5b2(1): nas bzhengs te// brjid pa dang bcas pas gar mdzad cing / zhal 'dzum pa dang 'dor ba dang / bskum pa dang / 'gying ba dang / spyan mdzes pas smin ring bskyod cing bsgyur ba dang / pad+mo phyag gis g.yas
5b3(1): g.yon gar gyi phreng ba'i tshul gyis sa'i ngos la zhabs 'phen cing bsgyur ba dang / 'dor zhing bskum pa dang / 'jog cing 'degs pa'i rnam par gnon pas nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du khyab par mdzad de/
5b4(1): rlung gi khams dang / me'i khams dang / chu'i khams dang / sa'i khams kun khyab par mdzad de/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub kyi sems la kun du khyab par mdzad de/ sna tshogs dang / phra ba dang / sgom pa dang /
5b5(1): bud med dang / gzhon nu dang / rgan pa dang / skyes pa dang / skyes pa ma yin pa dang / lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / skar ma dang / gshin rje dang / chu bdag dang / brgya byin dang / 'byung ba dang / 'byung ba
5b6(1): las gyur pa thams cad la bcom ldan 'das kun du bzang pos rgyas par byas te yang dag par gnas so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur te/ yang 'dus nas phyag
6a1(1): gar dang bcas nas thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das kun tu bzang po chen po la spyi bos btud nas gsol ba btab pa/ bcom ldan 'das kun gyi gsang ba'i he ru ka chen po rol pa'i thig le
6a2(1): 'di// gnyis med ye shes yang dag 'byung // bcom ldan khyod kyis bshad du gsol// sems can kun gyi ma skyes pa// skyes dang ma skyes rnam spangs pa'i// 'byung dang 'byung 'gyur rab sbyor pa'i// mchog tu rtag
6a3(1): pa'i sbyor ba'o// thams cad rin chen 'byung gnas dag/ nam mkha' dri med 'dra ba yi// rgyal mtshan chen po bsgreng bya ste// rdo rje chen pos dbang bskur ba'o// longs spyod chos ni yang dag 'byung // pad+mo'i mchog
6a4(1): ni dmar po mdog/ 'dod chags de nyid gsang ba che// bde byed thams cad bdud rtsi'i mchog/ la la ar ni don dang ldan// yang dag mdzes pa 'gying ba'i 'gros// sa phyogs ye shes bde ba che// byang chub
6a5(1): sems thig mchog nyid do// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa kun du bzang po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i bdag pos gsol ba btab pa mkhyen nas 'gog pa chen po ye shes
6a6(1): rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas cang mi gsung bar bzhugs so// de bzhin gshegs pa de dag ngo mtshar du gyur te// yang 'dus nas bcom ldan 'das dpal bde ba chen po kun du
6b1(1): bzang po chen po la de kho na nyid kyi dbyangs kyis bskul te bzhengs par mdzad do// oM AHhUM/ mi skye ye shes bde mchog ro la mnams// sems dpa'i mchog nyid 'gog pa rnams las bslang // chags med
6b2(1): kun du mya ngan 'das mdzad bzhengs shing mnams// mchog tu gsang ba'i dam bcas 'jig rten sgrol// byang chub skye gnas dbyings las gar mdzod cig/ sngon gyi nyon mongs rdo skams gzir ba yi// bde
6b3(1): mchog rgyan dang ldan pa'i thabs kyis bskul te go bar mdzad// de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal kun du bzang po chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po chen po he ru ka rol pa'i ting nge 'dzin la
6b4(1): snyoms par zhugs nas/ rang gis gsang ba'i thig le shin tu dgyes pa chen po zhes bya ba'i 'od zer gyi tshogs phyung nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i snying po'i thi le'i dbus su rgyas par
6b5(1): byas te/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du snang bar byas te/ steng dang 'og tu yang bzhugs te/ ma lus lus pa med pa'i ril dang / sems can thams cad la gsal bar byas nas shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i ro
6b6(1): bde ma mnyes par byas nas slar de nyid du slar log nas/ bcom ldan 'das shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i snying po gsang ba mchog gi thig le'i dbus na bzhugs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'od
7a1(1): zer gyi tshogs kyi phreng ba mchog tu bde bar gyur pa snying po des bskul ba ni gar mdzad cing rang rang gi ting nge 'dzin du dmigs nas bcom ldan 'das kun du bzang po chen po'i thugs kyi dbus
7a2(1): mchog tu gsang ba shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i bde bar bsgrubs te/ sku rang gi bud med kyi tshul du bskyed nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs ka nas mngon par 'byung bar gyur to/ de la la la ni spyan pad+ma lta
7a3(1): bur bskur cing smin dkyus ring // sangs rgyas tshul gyis gar mdzad pa'i// sangs rgyas rnal 'byor dkyil 'khor du// rab dgyes rdo rje gdon mi za// rdo rje sems la dgyes mdzad cing // bde ba'i sangs rgyas
7a4(1): bde ba yis// bcom ldan sangs rgyas bzhugs par 'gyur// zhal bsgyur smin ma bsgyur ba yis// spyan yang bskur zhing shin tu gnon// sor mo rnams kyang rab bsgyur dang // rdo rje tshul gyis gar mdzad
7a5(1): cing // sems dpa' che la mnyes par mdzad// rdo rje rnal 'byor ma dkyil du// sku ni skad cig bskul ba yis// bcom ldan rdo rje gnas par 'gyur// zhal ni brjid cing rin chen dbu// dri med spyi bor gar
7a6(1): mdzad cing // dkyil 'khor zhal gyis rnam bsgyur ba// byang chub sems ni med par mdzad// dur khrod yon tan tshogs dag gis// pad+ma'i spyan gyis gzigs mdzad cing // bde ba'i bdag po chen po la// rin
7b1(1): chen tshul gyis mnyes par mdzad// rab tu dgyes gsal bde ba yi// pad+ma dmar la che mdzad de// 'dod chags bral zhi rab tu bsgyur// pad+ma'i dra bas 'brel ba yi// pad+ma'i rnal 'byor ma dkyil du// brjid
7b2(1): pa'i spyan gyis kun gzigs pa'i// bde ba chen la mnyes par mdzad// bcom ldan pad+mo gnas par 'gyur// phyag gi sor mo rtse mo mtha'// rnam par bsgyur bar gar mdzad cing // phyag sbyar khong stong pad+ma
7b3(1): yis// glog bzhin dpral nas spyi gtsug tu// mchod pa'i sprin gyis longs spyod pas// sna tshogs bde byed gtso nyid la// las kyi tshul gyis mnyes mdzad cing // bcom ldan sna tshogs gnas par 'gyur// de
7b4(1): nas bcom ldan 'das kun du bzang po chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchog tu gsang ba byang chub sems kyi ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchog tu
7b5(1): gsang ba thig le byang chub kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyal po shin tu dgyes pa bde ba chen po nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // dkyil 'khor nyid kyi tshul gyis su// cho ga sbyor ba spros byas te// de
7b6(1): dang mthun pa'i dkyil 'khor gdon// sbyor ba'i gar gyis gar byas shing // ci ltar yang dag brtag par bya// ci ltar dkyil 'khor de kho na// he ru ka dpal dkyil 'khor ni// rdo rje sems dpa' dpa' bos
8a1(1): kyang // brtag par nus pa ma yin no// dkyil 'khor ye shes kyis brtags pas// snying po phyag rgya sngags rig gis// lha yi sbyor ba rgyas btab pas// cho ga shes pas bri bar bya// gru bzhi pa la sgra
8a2(1): bzhi pa// rta babs bzhi dang yang dag ldan// thig gis yongs su 'khor bar btab// dbus su 'khor lo rtsibs bzhir ldan// kun du yongs su mu khyud bcas// phyi rol rdo rje ra bas bskor// de'i dbus su
8a3(1): bcom ldan 'das che mchog he ru ka rigs bzhi he ru kas ni bskor// gra bzhi shwa ri yum dang bcas// de'i phyi rim 'khor lo rtsibs ni bcu drug la ye shes khro mo bcu drug/ de'i phyi rim pad+ma bcu drug la sprul pa'i
8a4(1): khro bo pha bcu drug/ de'i phyi rim pad+ma bcu drug la sprul pa'i phra men ma bcu drug de'i phyi rim snam bu gcig la yang sbrul bcu drug/ de'i phyi rim snam bu gcig la yang zhe sbrul bcu drug/ de'i phyi rol snam bu gcig
8a5(1): la sman gyi lha mo sum cu rtsa gnyis// de'i phyi rim snam bu la bcom ldan 'das de kho na nyid kyi sku bsil dpag bsam gyi shing bzhin/ de'i rtsa ba na sman bdud rtsi lhag ma re re/ gser gyi me tog gzhon nu re re/
8a6(1): bcom ldan 'das la mchod cing bdud rtsi bum pa thogs nas sku khrus mdzad pa re re/ de'i phyi rim snam bu la dbang phyug ma las las grub pa/ mgo brnyan ma nyi shu rtsa brgyad dgod// yang bcom ldan 'das kyi
8b1(1): dkyil 'khor gyi dgod pa'i don bzung zhing bka' stsal pa// dkyil 'khor gyi ni dbus nyid du// bcom ldan che mchog he ru ka/ dbu ni nyi shu rtsa gcig la// phyag ni bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis so// zhabs brgyad lha
8b2(1): chen pho mo mnan// glang chen ko rlon gos su gyon// zhing chen g.yang gzhi ya bskor// sbrul nag chun pos dbu la brgyan// thod pa rlon pas se ral kha// stag lpags mgo chen sham thabs can// khrag dang zhag gi
8b3(1): tshom bur bcas// bde gshegs rigs bzhi he ru ka/ khyu mchog ma he gzig dang stag/ mi 'jigs sems can bzhi yi khri// smug nag sngo nag ser nag dang // dmar nag ljang nag 'jigs pa'i
8b4(1): gzugs// dbu gsum phyag drug zhabs bzhir bgrad// cha lugs mgo bo yab dang mthun// dbus kyi dbu gyen du lta ba'i zhal gyi nang du rdo rje bcug nas gnyis su med pa'i sbyor ba tshul bzhin du mdzad cing
8b5(1): bzhugs so// rigs kyi yum kun gtso bo yab dang mthun// ye shes las grub pa'i khro bo rdo rje thogs med dang / khro bo rdo rje mdung dang / khro bo rdo rje me dpal dang / khro bo rdo rje mda' bsnyag dang / khro bo rdo rje
8b6(1): phur bu dang / khro bo rdo rje tho ba dang / khro bo rdo rje bya gri dang / khro bo rdo rje rnon po dang / khro bo rdo rje ral gri dang / khro bo rdo rje zhags pa dang / khro bo rdo rje gtun khung 'dzin dang / khro bo rdo rje gzhu 'dzin dang / khro bo rdo
